Career Fair - Join Us on April 24, 2026 from 1:00 p.m. to 4:00 p.m. at Delaware Technical Community College, Terry Campus, Del-One Conference Center, 100 Campus Drive, Dover, DE, 19904](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/events/images/career-fair-04242026.jpg)](https://degovforms.formstack.com/forms/career_fair_registration_april_2026)

## Application & Posting Status
  

#### Applications
You can view applications you have submitted or complete applications you have started by using the “My Applications” feature.
  * Complete an application, by selecting the “Finish” button next to the job.
  * Review completed application(s) or one for which the deadline has passed, by selecting the “Review” button next to the job.
  * View application notices, by selecting the “View” link under the “View Notices” column for that job.

  

[My Applications](https://www.jobapscloud.com/DE/newregpages/IDPassfind.asp?from=existing "View Applications")
  

#### Posting Status
The hiring agency will post information about the recruitment status on the “Status of Closed Postings” board. You can check the status of closed postings by:
  * Determine the Recruitment Number from your application
  * Find the Recruitment Number on the Status Board
  * Select the “Check Status” link

  

[Status of Closed Postings](https://www.jobapscloud.com/DE/statusboard.asp "View Applications")

## Your Future
  

The State of Delaware offers Comprehensive Retirement and Savings Plans to help **YOU** build a secure future.
  * [Pension Plan](https://open.omb.delaware.gov/)  
The State offers a generous pension. Employees become vested at ten (10) years of service.


  * [Correctional Officer Series](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/co/index.shtml)  
Employees in a Correctional Officer (CO) series position will be eligible to retire under the provisions of HB207 if they are employed as Hazardous Duty Level A-1 at the time of retirement, have completed twenty-five (25) years of pension creditable State service, and with at least twenty (20) of those years of pension creditable service as a CO series classified position as Hazardous Duty Level A-1.


  * [Deferred Compensation](https://treasurer.delaware.gov/deferred-compensation-plans/)  
Saving for retirement has never been easier or more cost effective. The State's deferred compensation plan provides employees with a means of building wealth for their futures in a flexible, easy to use and best of all tax deferred environment.

## Non-Merit Opportunities
  

What does the term “Non-Merit” mean? State of Delaware government positions in this category are not governed by a Merit System of Personnel Administration or the State of Delaware Merit Rules.
  
Non-Merit Opportunities  
---  
[Delaware National Guard](https://www.de.ng.mil/join/careers/) | [Judicial Branch](https://courts.delaware.gov/career/)  
[Delaware State Housing Authority](https://www.destatehousing.com/about/careers/) | [Justice, Department of](https://attorneygeneral.delaware.gov/executive/hr/career-opportunities/)  
[Delaware Technical & Community College](https://www.dtcc.edu/about/employment) | [Libraries, Division of](https://libraries.delaware.gov/)  
[Delaware Transit Corporation](https://candidate.dtc.deldot.gov/) | [Public Defender's Office](https://ods.delaware.gov/employment/)  
Education Non-Merit Opportunities  
---  
[Education, Department of](https://education.delaware.gov/about-doe/employment/) | [Education, Department of, Applicant Login](https://www.joindelawareschools.org/)  
  

[View List of Merit System Agencies](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/apply/job-types-merit.shtml#merit)

# Delaware Employment Link  
_Explore. Apply. Succeed._
  

### Overview of Application Services Menu
### [ Overview of Application Services Menu](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/apply/index.shtml#collapseOne)
  * #### [Application Services Home  ](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/apply/index.shtml)
  * #### [How to Apply ](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/apply/how.shtml)
  * #### [Application Status ](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/apply/application-status.shtml)
  * #### [Help Center ](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/apply/help-center.shtml)
  * #### [Practice Application ](https://jobapscloud.com/de/sup/bulpreview.asp?R1=PR0000&R2=000000&R3=010101)


## Work for Delaware
![Employ Your Ability, Find Your Opportunity Now](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/agency/img/job-opportunities.jpg)
  

Join the State of Delaware and do meaningful work that impacts your community every day. State employees enjoy a safe and inclusive work environment, a comprehensive benefits package, opportunities for personal and professional growth, paid leave, and the chance to touch people’s lives in a variety of ways.
  

### **How Do I Apply?**
  

#### [ **How to Apply** ](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/apply/how.shtml)
#### [ **Application Status** ](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/apply/application-status.shtml)
#### [ **Help Center** ](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/apply/help-center.shtml)
#### [ **Practice Application** ](https://jobapscloud.com/de/sup/bulpreview.asp?R1=PR0000&R2=000000&R3=010101)
### **Merit Jobs**
State of Delaware government agencies in this category are governed by a Merit System of Personnel Administration. Jobs that are classified as merit positions are subject to the Merit System Rules and Regulations.
[Merit Job Opportunities](https://www.jobapscloud.com/DE/)
[Merit System Rules and Regulations](https://merb.delaware.gov/state-merit-rules/)
### **Non-Merit Jobs**
State of Delaware government positions in this category are not governed by a Merit System of Personnel Administration or the State of Delaware Merit Rules.
[Non-Merit Job Opportunities](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/apply/job-types-non-merit.shtml)
[Non-Merit Education Job Opportunities](https://www.joindelawareschools.org/)
### **Casual/Seasonal Jobs**
State of Delaware government positions in this category may be employed by the State on a temporary basis and are not benefit eligible.
[Casual/Seasonal Job Opportunities](https://www.jobapscloud.com/DE/?Keyword=&Loc=&DeptNumber=&OccList=&JobType=CS&KeywordFullText=0)
### **Special Appointments**
There are four different types - Selective Placement, Return to Merit, Other Special Appointments, and Return to Work from a Disability
[Special Appointments](https://jobapscloud.com/de/sup/abfreenames.asp)

# Delaware Employment Link

![Job Seekers Image](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/agency/img/job-seekers-applicants.jpg)  

## Job Seekers
Find your future in the First State. From entry-level jobs to full career paths, the State of Delaware offers a wide range of occupations for job applicants. As a state employee, you have access to a comprehensive benefit package, training programs, paid leave, and the opportunity to positively impact the lives of Delawareans every day.
  

  

### **EXPLORE OUR RESOURCES**
#### [ **Resources for Applying** ](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/explore/application-resources.shtml)
#### [**Hiring Process** ](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/explore/hiring-process.shtml)
#### [ **Employment Resources** ](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/explore/employment-resources.shtml)
#### [ **Benefits** ](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/benefits/index.shtml)
#### [**People with Disabilities** ](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/disability/index.shtml)
#### [**Veterans** ](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/explore/veterans-preference.shtml)

## Law Enforcement / Public Safety Careers
  

#### **A job in Law Enforcement / Public Safety is more than a paycheck... It's a Career.**
We are looking for the best and brightest to become a member of the State of Delaware's Law Enforcement/Public Safety Team. A career in Law Enforcement/Public Safety is rewarding and we have a variety of career options. Start exploring today!
[![Correctional Officer](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/public-safety/images/corrections-cover.jpg)](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/corrections/co/index.shtml)
  

When you join the State of Delaware as a Correctional Officer, you will find tremendous promotional opportunities and your experiences will be far reaching.
[Correction](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/corrections/co/index.shtml)
[![Probation and Parole](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/public-safety/images/prob-parole-cover.jpg)](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/corrections/probation-parole/index.shtml)
  

As a Probation and Parole Officer, you will be responsible for overseeing people who have been convicted of a crime but are released on probation or parole.
[Probation and Parole](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/corrections/probation-parole/index.shtml)
[![Alcohol and Tobacco Enforcement](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/public-safety/images/dshs-date1.jpg)](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/homeland-security/ate/index.shtml)
  

Delaware Division of Alcohol and Tobacco Enforcement (ATE) is a state law enforcement agency.
[Alcohol & Tobacco](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/homeland-security/ate/index.shtml)
[![Delaware Capitol Police](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/public-safety/images/capitol-police.jpg)](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/homeland-security/dcp/index.shtml)
  

As a Capitol Police Officer you will provide law enforcement services to all branches of state government.
[Capitol Police](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/homeland-security/dcp/index.shtml)
[![DNREC Enforcement Officer](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/public-safety/images/dnrec-enforcement4.jpg)](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/dnrec/index.shtml)
  

As an Enforcement Officer, you will enforce natural resources, environmental, criminal, traffic, civil, & boating laws, rules, & regulations.
[Natural Resources](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/dnrec/index.shtml)
[![State Fire Marshal's Office](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/public-safety/images/sfm-burning-building.jpg)](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/fire/index.shtml)
  

The Office of the State Fire Marshal employs skilled and dedicated law enforcement officers titled Deputy Fire Marshals.
[Fire Marshal](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/fire/index.shtml)
[![Delaware State Police](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/public-safety/images/dsp.jpg)](https://dsp.delaware.gov/dsp_recruiting_become_a_trooper.shtml)
  

See the Delaware State Police website for trooper recruitment information.
[Delaware State Police](https://dsp.delaware.gov/dsp_recruiting_become_a_trooper.shtml)
  

There are so many possibilities and opportunities out there, so start applying today.

## Experience the Wonder and Diversity Delaware has to Offer
  

![Views from Beautiful Delaware](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/agency/img/location-images/location-animation.gif) Delaware is conveniently located on the eastern seaboard of the United States and is bordered by the Atlantic Ocean and the Delaware Bay, as well as by the states of New Jersey, Pennsylvania, and Maryland. Just a short drive takes you to New York, Philadelphia, Baltimore and Washington, DC. The Atlantic Ocean and the Delaware Bay offer many water-oriented attractions. Escape to “Chateau Country” for riveting landscapes, watch the sun rise over the ocean, visit the most beautifully preserved capitol complexes in the nation, exceptional bird watching, an extensive trail system for biking, hiking and canoeing, enjoy tax free shopping and much more.
From the Brandywine Valley to the Culinary Coast, come see what Delaware has to offer — we truly are “Not far from where you are.”
Explore more information about the State of Delaware at [Delaware Tourism](https://www.visitdelaware.com/) and [Relocating to Delaware](https://delaware.gov/guides/moving-to-delaware/).
Photos used by permission of the copyright holder who retains all rights.
Wilmington Waterfront, New Castle County, DE (photo courtesy of Paul Kennard)  
Rehoboth Beach, Sussex County, DE (photo courtesy of Mike Mahaffie)  
Dover Downs, Kent County, DE (photo courtesy of Mike DiCostanza)
Corn Field, Sussex County, DE (photo courtesy of Jeffrey Boyer)  
Wilmington Skyline, New Castle County, DE (photo courtesy of Mike DiCostanza)  
Lighthouse, Sussex County, DE (photo courtesy of David Gryte)

## Talent Acquisition
  

**“Our mission is to attract, select and retain a skilled workforce to provide quality services for Delaware's citizens, to increase self-service applications as a convenience for citizens, and to increase operational productivity.”**
The [Department of Human Resource Management](https://dhr.delaware.gov/), [Talent Acquisition](https://dhr.delaware.gov/talent-acquisition/index.shtml) invites you to search and apply for state government jobs using the Delaware Employment Link (DEL). Our goal is to link the right people with the right jobs where they can be part of building a better Delaware. 
Our Employment Service Office is here to help you if you need assistance or access to a computer.
Normal office hours are 8:00 a.m. to 4:30 p.m. Monday through Friday except on approved [Holidays](https://dhr.delaware.gov/labor/holidays/index.shtml).
  
Location | Phone / Fax  
---|---  
**New Castle County**  
13 Reads Way, Suite 202  
New Castle, DE 19720  
[Driving Directions](https://goo.gl/maps/rWT9X7HYPPNTCP9t6) | Phone: (302) 577-8977, option 2  
State Location Code: N705C  
Email: jobs@delaware.gov  
**Kent County**  
841 Silver Lake Boulevard, Suite 100  
Dover, DE 19904  
[Driving Directions](https://goo.gl/maps/oHSyruEHeR2xu4j16) | Phone: (302) 739-5458  
FAX: (302) 739-2327  
State Location Code: D702  
Email: jobs@delaware.gov  
Sussex County  
Georgetown |  Phone: (302) 856-5966  
Email: jobs@delaware.gov  
In addition, you can access a computer at local libraries and at [Department of Labor Career One-Stop Centers](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/documents/dol-onestop.pdf) around the State.
List of Public Libraries and Department of Labor [computer access sites](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/documents/computer-access.pdf) .

## Education Careers
  

![Join Delaware Schools](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/education/images/positively-delaware-teacher.jpg)
  

#### Consider a career in Teaching... Consider Delaware Schools
**Learning is life changing and you can impact our students...**
  

#### Become a Delaware Educator
Delaware district and charter schools are actively seeking educators interested in advancing educational excellence. We serve a diverse student population across our state and have a collective desire to provide equitable access to opportunities to help them succeed in college, career, and life. With more than 200 schools and 140,000 students, there’s an opportunity for everyone to find their place. We are proud of our achievements and strive every day to improve public education.
We are looking for dedicated professionals to fill a variety of positions both within and in support of schools — from teachers, paraprofessionals, central administrative office staff, and maintenance staff to school leaders and more. Our roles may vary, but one thing is always the same – our shared passion to have a meaningful impact on the lives of our students.
Delaware schools offer competitive salary and benefits packages for employees as well as many opportunities to grow professionally.
####  [Living in Delaware](https://www.visitdelaware.com/) - Experience the wonder and diversity Delaware has to offer.
  

#### Children Come First in the First State!
#### Find your next job here!

## Work for the Division of Youth Rehabilitative Services... _Be a hero._
  

[![Be a Hero and join the Division of Youth Rehabilitative Services!](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/youth-rehab/images/be-a-hero.jpg)](https://kids.delaware.gov/ "View Incentives at the Division of Youth Rehabilitative Services!") We at the Department of Services for Children, Youth, and Their Families know that Youth Rehabilitation, Family Service and Teacher positions play a huge role in empowering change in children’s lives. If you want a career in helping children and youth grow up safe and healthy – thriving physically, emotionally, and academically, you have come to the right place. Please join our team today!
The Department has more than 20 locations and serves over 8,000 children on any given day. As a Youth Rehabilitation Counselor (YRC), you will work in one of our rehabilitation programs or facilities and have the chance to make a positive impact on a youth’s rehabilitative journey, helping them grow and thrive once they leave our care.
[See the Youth Rehabilitation Career Path](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/youth-rehab/careerpath.shtml)
  

[![Youth Rehabilitation Counselor](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/youth-rehab/images/yrc.jpg)](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/youth-rehab/yrc-video.shtml)
[Youth Rehabilitation Counselor](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/youth-rehab/yrc-video.shtml)
  

#### Start your career journey today! Now offering a $10,000 Sign-On Bonus!
The Department of Services for Children, Youth and their Families (DSCYF) is now offering incentives for new hires for Teacher positions in accordance with the DSCYF Recruitment and Referral Program.
The program provides recruitment incentives as follows:
  * **$10,000 signing bonus** to full-time, Merit employees in the following classifications: Teacher, Teacher/Special Ed, or Teacher’s Aide. This bonus will be paid in **three installments** : $2,500 upon completing all required training, paperwork, and conditions of hire which is typically at three (3) months, $2,500 at twelve (12) months, and $5,000 after two full years (24 months) from the date of initial employment in a hard to position as identified above. [Sign On Incentive Flyer](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/youth-rehab/documents/signon-incentives.pdf)
  * $2,500 referral bonus to Merit DSCYF employees who refer applicants who become DSCYF new, full time, Teacher, Teacher Special Education or Teacher's Aide positions. The bonus will be paid in two installments: $1,250 upon form completion and applicant completing all conditions of hire and $1,250 paid 18 months after the new employee’s initial date of employment.


_NOTE: This program is administered by The Department of Services for Children, Youth and their Families. This program may be terminated by the State at any time. Casual-seasonal positions are not eligible for this program._
  

[Youth Rehabilitative Careers](https://www.jobapscloud.com/DE/?Keyword=youth%20rehabilitation&Loc=&DeptNumber=3700&OccList=&JobType=&KeywordFullText=0)

![Flexible work schedules + rewarding work.](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/img/masthead.jpg)
## Find your future in the First State
From entry-level jobs to full career paths, the State of Delaware offers a wide range of occupations for job applicants. As a state employee, you have access to a comprehensive benefit package, training programs, paid leave, and the opportunity to positively impact the lives of Delawareans every day.
### If you want to be a positive force and make an impact, we are hiring for all levels!
[Search All Jobs](https://www.jobapscloud.com/DE/ "Search All Jobs")
  * Excellent health benefits and retirements plans
  * Job security and flexibility in how you work
  * Ample time off and work/life balance
  * Opportunity for Public Service Loan Forgiveness
  * Best of all, you’ll do rewarding work that benefits our community
  * And now, with sign-on bonuses and referral incentives, there are more reasons than ever to join us.


## Featured Jobs
####  [ ![Health Careers - Stethoscope](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/img/stethoscope.svg) Healthcare Careers ](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/index.shtml#collapseHealthcare)
Your browser does not support the video tag. 
### Adding to the health of Delaware.
Healthcare careers with Delaware Health and Social Services and State Departments are full of positive outcomes, growth and rewards.
Here, you’ll be at very heart of nursing, where your work will help to promote the health and well-being of Delawareans who are most vulnerable and at risk. If you’re looking for a career as a CNA, LPN, RN, Nurse Supervisor, APN or Compliance Nurse where you can put your positives into practice, you’ll find it here in the First State.
Many of our nursing jobs offer exceptional rewards and incentives, such as:
  * Sign-on bonuses up to $5,000
  * Pension
  * Parental leave
  * Excellent health benefits
  * Earn up to $1,000 for referrals
  * Opportunity for Public Service Loan Forgiveness


[SEE ALL HEALTHCARE CAREERS](https://www.jobapscloud.com/DE/?Keyword=nurs&Loc=&DeptNumber=&OccList=&JobType=&KeywordFullText=0)
[Learn more about Healthcare Careers](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/nursing/index.shtml)
####  [ ![Corrections Careers - Badge](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/img/badge.svg) Department of Correction Careers ](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/index.shtml#collapseCorrections)
Your browser does not support the video tag. 
### Adding to the security and rehabilitation of inmates.
The teams working within the Delaware Department of Correction have the ability to turn something negative into something positive.
We bring our leadership skills, law enforcement training, compassion for people and conflict resolution abilities to our work every day to make our prisons safe, secure and humane centers of rehabilitation for our incarcerated populations.
Bring your positives to work within one of our featured DOC jobs, including Correctional Officers, Canine Handlers, Maintenance Workers and Food Service professionals. See all the good that comes from a career in Corrections with the First State, including:
  * Sign-on bonuses up to $5,000
  * Earn up to $2,000 for referrals
  * Tremendous opportunities for promotion
  * A 25-year pension plan
  * Parental leave
  * Excellent health benefits


[SEE ALL CORRECTIONAL CAREERS](https://www.jobapscloud.com/DE/?Keyword=&Loc=&DeptNumber=3800&OccList=&JobType=&KeywordFullText=0)
[Learn more about Correctional Careers](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/corrections/co/index.shtml)
####  [ ![Careers Working with Children, Youth, and Familes](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/img/blocks.svg) Children, Youth and Their Families Careers ](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/index.shtml#collapseChildren)
Your browser does not support the video tag. 
### Adding to stronger families and brighter futures.
The teams working within the Delaware Department of Services for Children, Youth, and Their Families are enhancing communities one family and one child at a time.
All of this adds up to strong communities, safe and healthy children and resilient families.
Bring your positives to work within one of our featured family service or youth rehabilitation jobs. See all the good that comes from family-focused career with the First State, including:
  * Parental leave
  * Excellent health benefits
  * Pension plan
  * Opportunity for Public Service Loan Forgiveness


[SEE ALL YOUTH AND FAMILY SERVICE CAREERS](https://www.jobapscloud.com/DE/?Keyword=&Loc=&DeptNumber=3700&OccList=12&JobType=&KeywordFullText=0%20)
[Learn more about Youth and Family Service Careers](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/youth-rehab/index.shtml)
####  [ ![Engineering Careers](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/img/gears.svg) Engineering Careers ](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/index.shtml#collapseEngineering)
Your browser does not support the video tag. 
### Adding to a better Delaware.
Engineers within Delaware’s Department of Transportation and Department of Natural Resources and Environmental Control are building a better state with visionary work that has a positive impact on our environment, natural beauty and daily life of Delawareans. We offer rewarding careers for a full array of engineering disciplines including civil, environmental, electrical, materials, chemical and mechanical engineering.
Bring your positives to work with one of our featured Engineering jobs. See all the good that comes from your career with the First State, including:
  * Sign-on bonuses up to $7,000
  * Excellent health benefits
  * Parental leave
  * Pension plan
  * Opportunity for Public Service Loan Forgiveness


[SEE ALL ENGINEERING CAREERS](https://www.jobapscloud.com/DE/?Keyword=&Loc=&DeptNumber=&OccList=19&JobType=&KeywordFullText=0)
[Learn more about Engineering Careers](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/engineering/index.shtml)
####  [ ![HVAC](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/img/hvac.svg) HVAC Careers ](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/index.shtml#collapseHVAC)
Your browser does not support the video tag. 
### Adding to the comfort of our work force.
As an HVAC/Refrigeration Technician within the Delaware Office of Management and Budget, you’ll make life a lot more comfortable for your colleagues while you make a comfortable living with positive growth potential and incentives including:
  * Sign-on bonus of $3,000*
  * Excellent health benefits
  * Parental leave
  * Pension plan
  * Earn $1,000 for referrals*


*Sign-on bonus and referral bonus applicable to New Castle County positions only
[SEE ALL HVAC/REFRIGERATION TECHNICIAN CAREERS](https://www.jobapscloud.com/DE/?Keyword=HVAC&Loc=&DeptNumber=&OccList=&JobType=&KeywordFullText=0)

# Delaware Employment Link  
_Explore. Apply. Succeed._
  

![Image](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/mstn/images/header-new2.jpg)
![Military person tying their boots](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/mstn/images/boots.jpg)
  

[Connect with Us!](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/index.shtml)
[![Facebook](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/img/CLF_sm_facebook_U9.png)](https://facebook.com/DEStateJobs) [![Instagram](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/img/CLF_sm_instagram_U9.png)](https://instagram.com/delawarestatejobs/) [![Twitter](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/img/CLF_sm_twitter_U9.png)](https://twitter.com/DEStateJobs) [![YouTube](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/img/CLF_sm_youtube_U9.png)](https://www.youtube.com/channel/UCzVfs-N-tYOdyFX3QmE_Y7A) [![Linkedin](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/img/CLF_sm_linkedIn_U9.png)](https://www.linkedin.com/company/state-of-delaware) [![glassdoor](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/img/CLF_sm_glassdoor_U9.png)](https://www.glassdoor.com/Overview/Working-at-State-of-Delaware-EI_IE310774.11,28.htm)
  

### Program Overview
Open to all identified military spouses working for state government agencies in NASPE member states.  
The program activates when a military spouse/state employee receives notification of a Permanent Change of Station (PCS).  
The program is designed to deliver career services such as resume review/building, skills translation, informal contacts, etc. in support of military spouse re-employment.
### **Change can be hard, but it doesn't have to be.**
#### **The State of Delaware's Military Spouse Transition Network is here to help.**
  

### Why the need?
Military spouses change duty stations, moving across the country approximately every three years. This has a major impact on their careers and their ability to provide financial support to their family.
### The Result
Most working military spouses are forced to either take minimum-wage jobs that do not have long-term career options (e.g. retail, service, etc.) or start from the bottom in their chosen career field each time they move.
### Making Moves
As a transitioning Military Spouse you will begin by connecting with your [MSTN State Representative](https://naspe.memberclicks.net/index.php?option=com_mcsearchresults&view=search&uuid=8f2cfde5-31f9-40c5-a01a-53523c74b53f#!/) to conduct an official intake meeting to do a review of your resume, interviewing skills, and identify jobs that align with your experience and/or personal interest.
Upon completion of the initial intake meeting, the “Home” state MSTN Representative will initiate contact with the “Receiving” states MSTN Representative to share your name and contact information, as well as a copy of your current resume. They may also provide you with the “Receiving” states MSTN Website information where you can submit an [Inquiry Form](https://degovforms.formstack.com/forms/mstn_inquiry) to establish contact on your own!
The “Receiving” state will schedule a meeting to review the details provided and begin translating your skills to align with the most appropriate classification system for consideration. A thorough review of the state’s resources will also be provided, ensuring you are fully prepared to embark on the employment journey in your new home state!
* * *

## **Ready to get started?**

All Military Dependents are welcome to submit an Inquiry Form to learn more about our opportunities.  
The State of Delaware is eager to serve any and all Military families in any way that we can. We look forward to hearing from you soon!

## Application & Posting Status
  

#### Applications
You can view applications you have submitted or complete applications you have started by using the “My Applications” feature.
  * Complete an application, by selecting the “Finish” button next to the job.
  * Review completed application(s) or one for which the deadline has passed, by selecting the “Review” button next to the job.
  * View application notices, by selecting the “View” link under the “View Notices” column for that job.

  

[My Applications](https://www.jobapscloud.com/DE/newregpages/IDPassfind.asp?from=existing "View Applications")
  

#### Posting Status
The hiring agency will post information about the recruitment status on the “Status of Closed Postings” board. You can check the status of closed postings by:
  * Determine the Recruitment Number from your application
  * Find the Recruitment Number on the Status Board
  * Select the “Check Status” link

  

[Status of Closed Postings](https://www.jobapscloud.com/DE/statusboard.asp "View Applications")

## Education Careers
  

![Join Delaware Schools](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/education/images/positively-delaware-teacher.jpg)
  

#### Consider a career in Teaching... Consider Delaware Schools
**Learning is life changing and you can impact our students...**
  

#### Become a Delaware Educator
Delaware district and charter schools are actively seeking educators interested in advancing educational excellence. We serve a diverse student population across our state and have a collective desire to provide equitable access to opportunities to help them succeed in college, career, and life. With more than 200 schools and 140,000 students, there’s an opportunity for everyone to find their place. We are proud of our achievements and strive every day to improve public education.
We are looking for dedicated professionals to fill a variety of positions both within and in support of schools — from teachers, paraprofessionals, central administrative office staff, and maintenance staff to school leaders and more. Our roles may vary, but one thing is always the same – our shared passion to have a meaningful impact on the lives of our students.
Delaware schools offer competitive salary and benefits packages for employees as well as many opportunities to grow professionally.
####  [Living in Delaware](https://www.visitdelaware.com/) - Experience the wonder and diversity Delaware has to offer.
  

#### Children Come First in the First State!
#### Find your next job here!
  

[ **Why Delaware** ](https://www.joindelawareschools.org/why-delaware/)   
[ ![Teaching in Delaware](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/education/images/education1a.jpg) ](https://www.joindelawareschools.org/why-delaware/)
  

[ **Becoming a DE Educator** ](https://www.joindelawareschools.org/become-an-educator/)   
[ ![Becoming a Delaware Educator](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/education/images/education2a.jpg) ](https://www.joindelawareschools.org/become-an-educator/)

## Non-Merit Opportunities
  

What does the term “Non-Merit” mean? State of Delaware government positions in this category are not governed by a Merit System of Personnel Administration or the State of Delaware Merit Rules.
  
Non-Merit Opportunities  
---  
[Delaware National Guard](https://www.de.ng.mil/join/careers/) | [Judicial Branch](https://courts.delaware.gov/career/)  
[Delaware State Housing Authority](https://www.destatehousing.com/about/careers/) | [Justice, Department of](https://attorneygeneral.delaware.gov/executive/hr/career-opportunities/)  
[Delaware Technical & Community College](https://www.dtcc.edu/about/employment) | [Libraries, Division of](https://libraries.delaware.gov/)  
[Delaware Transit Corporation](https://candidate.dtc.deldot.gov/) | [Public Defender's Office](https://ods.delaware.gov/employment/)  
Education Non-Merit Opportunities  
---  
[Education, Department of](https://education.delaware.gov/about-doe/employment/) | [Education, Department of, Applicant Login](https://www.joindelawareschools.org/)  
  

[View List of Merit System Agencies](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/apply/job-types-merit.shtml#merit)

# Delaware Employment Link   
_Explore. Apply. Succeed._
  

![Flexible work schedules + rewarding work.](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/img/masthead.jpg)
## Find your future in the First State
From entry-level jobs to full career paths, the State of Delaware offers a wide range of occupations for job applicants. As a state employee, you have access to a comprehensive benefit package, training programs, paid leave, and the opportunity to positively impact the lives of Delawareans every day.
### If you want to be a positive force and make an impact, we are hiring for all levels!
[Search All Jobs](https://www.jobapscloud.com/DE/ "Search All Jobs")
  * Excellent health benefits and retirements plans
  * Job security and flexibility in how you work
  * Ample time off and work/life balance
  * Opportunity for Public Service Loan Forgiveness
  * Best of all, you’ll do rewarding work that benefits our community
  * And now, with sign-on bonuses and referral incentives, there are more reasons than ever to join us.


## Featured Jobs
####  [ ![Health Careers - Stethoscope](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/img/stethoscope.svg) Healthcare Careers ](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/index.shtml#collapseHealthcare)
Your browser does not support the video tag. 
### Adding to the health of Delaware.
Healthcare careers with Delaware Health and Social Services and State Departments are full of positive outcomes, growth and rewards.
Here, you’ll be at very heart of nursing, where your work will help to promote the health and well-being of Delawareans who are most vulnerable and at risk. If you’re looking for a career as a CNA, LPN, RN, Nurse Supervisor, APN or Compliance Nurse where you can put your positives into practice, you’ll find it here in the First State.
Many of our nursing jobs offer exceptional rewards and incentives, such as:
  * Sign-on bonuses up to $5,000
  * Pension
  * Parental leave
  * Excellent health benefits
  * Earn up to $1,000 for referrals
  * Opportunity for Public Service Loan Forgiveness


[SEE ALL HEALTHCARE CAREERS](https://www.jobapscloud.com/DE/?Keyword=nurs&Loc=&DeptNumber=&OccList=&JobType=&KeywordFullText=0)
[Learn more about Healthcare Careers](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/nursing/index.shtml)
####  [ ![Corrections Careers - Badge](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/img/badge.svg) Department of Correction Careers ](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/index.shtml#collapseCorrections)
Your browser does not support the video tag. 
### Adding to the security and rehabilitation of inmates.
The teams working within the Delaware Department of Correction have the ability to turn something negative into something positive.
We bring our leadership skills, law enforcement training, compassion for people and conflict resolution abilities to our work every day to make our prisons safe, secure and humane centers of rehabilitation for our incarcerated populations.
Bring your positives to work within one of our featured DOC jobs, including Correctional Officers, Canine Handlers, Maintenance Workers and Food Service professionals. See all the good that comes from a career in Corrections with the First State, including:
  * Sign-on bonuses up to $5,000
  * Earn up to $2,000 for referrals
  * Tremendous opportunities for promotion
  * A 25-year pension plan
  * Parental leave
  * Excellent health benefits


[SEE ALL CORRECTIONAL CAREERS](https://www.jobapscloud.com/DE/?Keyword=&Loc=&DeptNumber=3800&OccList=&JobType=&KeywordFullText=0)
[Learn more about Correctional Careers](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/corrections/co/index.shtml)
####  [ ![Careers Working with Children, Youth, and Familes](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/img/blocks.svg) Children, Youth and Their Families Careers ](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/index.shtml#collapseChildren)
Your browser does not support the video tag. 
### Adding to stronger families and brighter futures.
The teams working within the Delaware Department of Services for Children, Youth, and Their Families are enhancing communities one family and one child at a time.
All of this adds up to strong communities, safe and healthy children and resilient families.
Bring your positives to work within one of our featured family service or youth rehabilitation jobs. See all the good that comes from family-focused career with the First State, including:
  * Parental leave
  * Excellent health benefits
  * Pension plan
  * Opportunity for Public Service Loan Forgiveness


[SEE ALL YOUTH AND FAMILY SERVICE CAREERS](https://www.jobapscloud.com/DE/?Keyword=&Loc=&DeptNumber=3700&OccList=12&JobType=&KeywordFullText=0%20)
[Learn more about Youth and Family Service Careers](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/youth-rehab/index.shtml)
####  [ ![Engineering Careers](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/img/gears.svg) Engineering Careers ](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/index.shtml#collapseEngineering)
Your browser does not support the video tag. 
### Adding to a better Delaware.
Engineers within Delaware’s Department of Transportation and Department of Natural Resources and Environmental Control are building a better state with visionary work that has a positive impact on our environment, natural beauty and daily life of Delawareans. We offer rewarding careers for a full array of engineering disciplines including civil, environmental, electrical, materials, chemical and mechanical engineering.
Bring your positives to work with one of our featured Engineering jobs. See all the good that comes from your career with the First State, including:
  * Sign-on bonuses up to $7,000
  * Excellent health benefits
  * Parental leave
  * Pension plan
  * Opportunity for Public Service Loan Forgiveness


[SEE ALL ENGINEERING CAREERS](https://www.jobapscloud.com/DE/?Keyword=&Loc=&DeptNumber=&OccList=19&JobType=&KeywordFullText=0)
[Learn more about Engineering Careers](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/engineering/index.shtml)
####  [ ![HVAC](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/img/hvac.svg) HVAC Careers ](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/index.shtml#collapseHVAC)
Your browser does not support the video tag. 
### Adding to the comfort of our work force.
As an HVAC/Refrigeration Technician within the Delaware Office of Management and Budget, you’ll make life a lot more comfortable for your colleagues while you make a comfortable living with positive growth potential and incentives including:
  * Sign-on bonus of $3,000*
  * Excellent health benefits
  * Parental leave
  * Pension plan
  * Earn $1,000 for referrals*


*Sign-on bonus and referral bonus applicable to New Castle County positions only
[SEE ALL HVAC/REFRIGERATION TECHNICIAN CAREERS](https://www.jobapscloud.com/DE/?Keyword=HVAC&Loc=&DeptNumber=&OccList=&JobType=&KeywordFullText=0)

## Your Future
  

The State of Delaware offers Comprehensive Retirement and Savings Plans to help **YOU** build a secure future.
  * [Pension Plan](https://open.omb.delaware.gov/)  
The State offers a generous pension. Employees become vested at ten (10) years of service.


  * [Correctional Officer Series](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/co/index.shtml)  
Employees in a Correctional Officer (CO) series position will be eligible to retire under the provisions of HB207 if they are employed as Hazardous Duty Level A-1 at the time of retirement, have completed twenty-five (25) years of pension creditable State service, and with at least twenty (20) of those years of pension creditable service as a CO series classified position as Hazardous Duty Level A-1.


  * [Deferred Compensation](https://treasurer.delaware.gov/deferred-compensation-plans/)  
Saving for retirement has never been easier or more cost effective. The State's deferred compensation plan provides employees with a means of building wealth for their futures in a flexible, easy to use and best of all tax deferred environment.

## Law Enforcement / Public Safety Careers
  

#### **A job in Law Enforcement / Public Safety is more than a paycheck... It's a Career.**
We are looking for the best and brightest to become a member of the State of Delaware's Law Enforcement/Public Safety Team. A career in Law Enforcement/Public Safety is rewarding and we have a variety of career options. Start exploring today!
[![Correctional Officer](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/public-safety/images/corrections-cover.jpg)](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/corrections/co/index.shtml)
  

When you join the State of Delaware as a Correctional Officer, you will find tremendous promotional opportunities and your experiences will be far reaching.
[Correction](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/corrections/co/index.shtml)
[![Probation and Parole](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/public-safety/images/prob-parole-cover.jpg)](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/corrections/probation-parole/index.shtml)
  

As a Probation and Parole Officer, you will be responsible for overseeing people who have been convicted of a crime but are released on probation or parole.
[Probation and Parole](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/corrections/probation-parole/index.shtml)
[![Alcohol and Tobacco Enforcement](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/public-safety/images/dshs-date1.jpg)](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/homeland-security/ate/index.shtml)
  

Delaware Division of Alcohol and Tobacco Enforcement (ATE) is a state law enforcement agency.
[Alcohol & Tobacco](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/homeland-security/ate/index.shtml)
[![Delaware Capitol Police](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/public-safety/images/capitol-police.jpg)](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/homeland-security/dcp/index.shtml)
  

As a Capitol Police Officer you will provide law enforcement services to all branches of state government.
[Capitol Police](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/homeland-security/dcp/index.shtml)
[![DNREC Enforcement Officer](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/public-safety/images/dnrec-enforcement4.jpg)](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/dnrec/index.shtml)
  

As an Enforcement Officer, you will enforce natural resources, environmental, criminal, traffic, civil, & boating laws, rules, & regulations.
[Natural Resources](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/dnrec/index.shtml)
[![State Fire Marshal's Office](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/public-safety/images/sfm-burning-building.jpg)](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/fire/index.shtml)
  

The Office of the State Fire Marshal employs skilled and dedicated law enforcement officers titled Deputy Fire Marshals.
[Fire Marshal](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/fire/index.shtml)
[![Delaware State Police](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/public-safety/images/dsp.jpg)](https://dsp.delaware.gov/dsp_recruiting_become_a_trooper.shtml)
  

See the Delaware State Police website for trooper recruitment information.
[Delaware State Police](https://dsp.delaware.gov/dsp_recruiting_become_a_trooper.shtml)
  

There are so many possibilities and opportunities out there, so start applying today.

# Delaware Employment Link  
_Explore. Apply. Succeed._
  

### Overview of Application Services Menu
### [ Overview of Application Services Menu](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/apply/index.shtml#collapseOne)
  * #### [Application Services Home  ](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/apply/index.shtml)
  * #### [How to Apply ](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/apply/how.shtml)
  * #### [Application Status ](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/apply/application-status.shtml)
  * #### [Help Center ](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/apply/help-center.shtml)
  * #### [Practice Application ](https://jobapscloud.com/de/sup/bulpreview.asp?R1=PR0000&R2=000000&R3=010101)


## Work for Delaware
![Employ Your Ability, Find Your Opportunity Now](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/agency/img/job-opportunities.jpg)
  

Join the State of Delaware and do meaningful work that impacts your community every day. State employees enjoy a safe and inclusive work environment, a comprehensive benefits package, opportunities for personal and professional growth, paid leave, and the chance to touch people’s lives in a variety of ways.
  

### **How Do I Apply?**
  

#### [ **How to Apply** ](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/apply/how.shtml)
#### [ **Application Status** ](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/apply/application-status.shtml)
#### [ **Help Center** ](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/apply/help-center.shtml)
#### [ **Practice Application** ](https://jobapscloud.com/de/sup/bulpreview.asp?R1=PR0000&R2=000000&R3=010101)
### **Merit Jobs**
State of Delaware government agencies in this category are governed by a Merit System of Personnel Administration. Jobs that are classified as merit positions are subject to the Merit System Rules and Regulations.
[Merit Job Opportunities](https://www.jobapscloud.com/DE/)
[Merit System Rules and Regulations](https://merb.delaware.gov/state-merit-rules/)
### **Non-Merit Jobs**
State of Delaware government positions in this category are not governed by a Merit System of Personnel Administration or the State of Delaware Merit Rules.
[Non-Merit Job Opportunities](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/apply/job-types-non-merit.shtml)
[Non-Merit Education Job Opportunities](https://www.joindelawareschools.org/)
### **Casual/Seasonal Jobs**
State of Delaware government positions in this category may be employed by the State on a temporary basis and are not benefit eligible.
[Casual/Seasonal Job Opportunities](https://www.jobapscloud.com/DE/?Keyword=&Loc=&DeptNumber=&OccList=&JobType=CS&KeywordFullText=0)
### **Special Appointments**
There are four different types - Selective Placement, Return to Merit, Other Special Appointments, and Return to Work from a Disability
[Special Appointments](https://jobapscloud.com/de/sup/abfreenames.asp)

## Work for the Division of Youth Rehabilitative Services... _Be a hero._
  

[![Be a Hero and join the Division of Youth Rehabilitative Services!](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/youth-rehab/images/be-a-hero.jpg)](https://kids.delaware.gov/ "View Incentives at the Division of Youth Rehabilitative Services!") We at the Department of Services for Children, Youth, and Their Families know that Youth Rehabilitation, Family Service and Teacher positions play a huge role in empowering change in children’s lives. If you want a career in helping children and youth grow up safe and healthy – thriving physically, emotionally, and academically, you have come to the right place. Please join our team today!
The Department has more than 20 locations and serves over 8,000 children on any given day. As a Youth Rehabilitation Counselor (YRC), you will work in one of our rehabilitation programs or facilities and have the chance to make a positive impact on a youth’s rehabilitative journey, helping them grow and thrive once they leave our care.
[See the Youth Rehabilitation Career Path](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/youth-rehab/careerpath.shtml)
  

[![Youth Rehabilitation Counselor](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/youth-rehab/images/yrc.jpg)](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/youth-rehab/yrc-video.shtml)
[Youth Rehabilitation Counselor](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/youth-rehab/yrc-video.shtml)
  

#### Start your career journey today! Now offering a $10,000 Sign-On Bonus!
The Department of Services for Children, Youth and their Families (DSCYF) is now offering incentives for new hires for Teacher positions in accordance with the DSCYF Recruitment and Referral Program.
The program provides recruitment incentives as follows:
  * **$10,000 signing bonus** to full-time, Merit employees in the following classifications: Teacher, Teacher/Special Ed, or Teacher’s Aide. This bonus will be paid in **three installments** : $2,500 upon completing all required training, paperwork, and conditions of hire which is typically at three (3) months, $2,500 at twelve (12) months, and $5,000 after two full years (24 months) from the date of initial employment in a hard to position as identified above. [Sign On Incentive Flyer](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/careers/youth-rehab/documents/signon-incentives.pdf)
  * $2,500 referral bonus to Merit DSCYF employees who refer applicants who become DSCYF new, full time, Teacher, Teacher Special Education or Teacher's Aide positions. The bonus will be paid in two installments: $1,250 upon form completion and applicant completing all conditions of hire and $1,250 paid 18 months after the new employee’s initial date of employment.


_NOTE: This program is administered by The Department of Services for Children, Youth and their Families. This program may be terminated by the State at any time. Casual-seasonal positions are not eligible for this program._

## Experience the Wonder and Diversity Delaware has to Offer
  

![Views from Beautiful Delaware](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/agency/img/location-images/location-animation.gif) Delaware is conveniently located on the eastern seaboard of the United States and is bordered by the Atlantic Ocean and the Delaware Bay, as well as by the states of New Jersey, Pennsylvania, and Maryland. Just a short drive takes you to New York, Philadelphia, Baltimore and Washington, DC. The Atlantic Ocean and the Delaware Bay offer many water-oriented attractions. Escape to “Chateau Country” for riveting landscapes, watch the sun rise over the ocean, visit the most beautifully preserved capitol complexes in the nation, exceptional bird watching, an extensive trail system for biking, hiking and canoeing, enjoy tax free shopping and much more.
From the Brandywine Valley to the Culinary Coast, come see what Delaware has to offer — we truly are “Not far from where you are.”
Explore more information about the State of Delaware at [Delaware Tourism](https://www.visitdelaware.com/) and [Relocating to Delaware](https://delaware.gov/guides/moving-to-delaware/).

# Delaware Employment Link  
_Explore. Apply. Succeed._
  

## Talent Acquisition
  

**“Our mission is to attract, select and retain a skilled workforce to provide quality services for Delaware's citizens, to increase self-service applications as a convenience for citizens, and to increase operational productivity.”**
The [Department of Human Resource Management](https://dhr.delaware.gov/), [Talent Acquisition](https://dhr.delaware.gov/talent-acquisition/index.shtml) invites you to search and apply for state government jobs using the Delaware Employment Link (DEL). Our goal is to link the right people with the right jobs where they can be part of building a better Delaware. 
Our Employment Service Office is here to help you if you need assistance or access to a computer.
Normal office hours are 8:00 a.m. to 4:30 p.m. Monday through Friday except on approved [Holidays](https://dhr.delaware.gov/labor/holidays/index.shtml).
  
Location | Phone / Fax  
---|---  
**New Castle County**  
13 Reads Way, Suite 202  
New Castle, DE 19720  
[Driving Directions](https://goo.gl/maps/rWT9X7HYPPNTCP9t6) | Phone: (302) 577-8977, option 2  
State Location Code: N705C  
Email: jobs@delaware.gov  
**Kent County**  
841 Silver Lake Boulevard, Suite 100  
Dover, DE 19904  
[Driving Directions](https://goo.gl/maps/oHSyruEHeR2xu4j16) | Phone: (302) 739-5458  
FAX: (302) 739-2327  
State Location Code: D702  
Email: jobs@delaware.gov  
Sussex County  
Georgetown |  Phone: (302) 856-5966  
Email: jobs@delaware.gov  
In addition, you can access a computer at local libraries and at [Department of Labor Career One-Stop Centers](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/documents/dol-onestop.pdf) around the State.
List of Public Libraries and Department of Labor [computer access sites](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/documents/computer-access.pdf) .

# Delaware Employment Link  
_Explore. Apply. Succeed._
  

![Image](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/mstn/images/header-new2.jpg)
![Military person tying their boots](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/mstn/images/boots.jpg)
  

[Connect with Us!](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/index.shtml)
[![Facebook](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/img/CLF_sm_facebook_U9.png)](https://facebook.com/DEStateJobs) [![Instagram](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/img/CLF_sm_instagram_U9.png)](https://instagram.com/delawarestatejobs/) [![Twitter](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/img/CLF_sm_twitter_U9.png)](https://twitter.com/DEStateJobs) [![YouTube](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/img/CLF_sm_youtube_U9.png)](https://www.youtube.com/channel/UCzVfs-N-tYOdyFX3QmE_Y7A) [![Linkedin](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/img/CLF_sm_linkedIn_U9.png)](https://www.linkedin.com/company/state-of-delaware) [![glassdoor](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/img/CLF_sm_glassdoor_U9.png)](https://www.glassdoor.com/Overview/Working-at-State-of-Delaware-EI_IE310774.11,28.htm)
  

### Program Overview
Open to all identified military spouses working for state government agencies in NASPE member states.  
The program activates when a military spouse/state employee receives notification of a Permanent Change of Station (PCS).  
The program is designed to deliver career services such as resume review/building, skills translation, informal contacts, etc. in support of military spouse re-employment.
### **Change can be hard, but it doesn't have to be.**
#### **The State of Delaware's Military Spouse Transition Network is here to help.**
  

### Why the need?
Military spouses change duty stations, moving across the country approximately every three years. This has a major impact on their careers and their ability to provide financial support to their family.
### The Result
Most working military spouses are forced to either take minimum-wage jobs that do not have long-term career options (e.g. retail, service, etc.) or start from the bottom in their chosen career field each time they move.
### Making Moves
As a transitioning Military Spouse you will begin by connecting with your [MSTN State Representative](https://naspe.memberclicks.net/index.php?option=com_mcsearchresults&view=search&uuid=8f2cfde5-31f9-40c5-a01a-53523c74b53f#!/) to conduct an official intake meeting to do a review of your resume, interviewing skills, and identify jobs that align with your experience and/or personal interest.
Upon completion of the initial intake meeting, the “Home” state MSTN Representative will initiate contact with the “Receiving” states MSTN Representative to share your name and contact information, as well as a copy of your current resume. They may also provide you with the “Receiving” states MSTN Website information where you can submit an [Inquiry Form](https://degovforms.formstack.com/forms/mstn_inquiry) to establish contact on your own!
The “Receiving” state will schedule a meeting to review the details provided and begin translating your skills to align with the most appropriate classification system for consideration. A thorough review of the state’s resources will also be provided, ensuring you are fully prepared to embark on the employment journey in your new home state!
* * *

## **Ready to get started?**
### **[Submit an Inquiry Form Here](https://degovforms.formstack.com/forms/mstn_inquiry)**

All Military Dependents are welcome to submit an Inquiry Form to learn more about our opportunities.  
The State of Delaware is eager to serve any and all Military families in any way that we can. We look forward to hearing from you soon!

# Delaware Employment Link  
_Explore. Apply. Succeed._
  

  

![Job Seekers Image](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/agency/img/job-seekers-applicants.jpg)  

## Job Seekers
Find your future in the First State. From entry-level jobs to full career paths, the State of Delaware offers a wide range of occupations for job applicants. As a state employee, you have access to a comprehensive benefit package, training programs, paid leave, and the opportunity to positively impact the lives of Delawareans every day.
  

  

### **EXPLORE OUR RESOURCES**
#### [ **Resources for Applying** ](https://statejobs.delaware.gov/explore/application-resources.shtml)

* * *
The State of Delaware is an Equal Opportunity employer and values a diverse workforce. We strongly encourage and seek out a workforce representative of Delaware including race, color, religion, age, sex, national origin, disability status, genetics, protected veteran status, sexual orientation, gender identity or expression.
